    🚀 The system is made up of Producers (who produce events) and Consumers (who process the events).

    Posted on: 2023-02-10; at: 11:25

    ✔️ Standardize technology, patterns, SRE & auditing, data governance, and reliability for fault tolerance and event reprocessing.

    Posted on: 2023-02-10; at: 11:25

    💬 Event-driven micro-services allows real-time communication and data consumption in the form of events.
